name:S‚Äçi‚Äçl‚Äçe‚Äçn‚Äçc‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçk‚Äçy‚Äçs
info:Deluxe Suite Red Level
info:Stayed in March 2024
info:Solo travelers
info:62 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted April 2, 2024
msg:Gran Melia is the top luxury brand of the Spanish Meli√° Group, but the two domestic hotels are in line with local customs and adopt the design of imitating Tang Dynasty palace architecture. When placed in Xi'an, it also echoes the city's tone. The location of the hotel is still very good, close to Qujiang Lake, and some rooms can see the Qujiang landscape.
.
The hotel lobby is high and spacious, with a mountain-shaped roof and a glass dome design, which has good light transmittance, so the scenery in the lobby is very transparent during the day, and it is two different styles at night, and it is also very photogenic.
.
There is a pre-check-in call, and the concierge service is also very good. In terms of overall service level, it is better than the Gran Melia Chengdu, and even better than the Qujiang Hyatt with a similar style, which is quite surprising to me.
.
Because the Melia Group does not have a very powerful membership system, I directly booked the Shengshi Hongge Huanxiang Suite this time. The area is nominally 103 square meters. It is on the 5th floor, the highest floor of the hotel, and is very close to the executive lounge. This floor is considered the hotel's executive floor. The room is very high and comfortable. The only flaw is that this suite is already the second-highest room type in the hotel, but there is basically no view outside the window.
.
The suite has a square floor plan, with one bedroom, one living room, two bathrooms and one cloakroom. There is a balcony but the area is not large, so you can only take a walk. There is a side cabinet on the left hand side of the door for storing sundries, and a guest bathroom on the right hand side, which is quite spacious.
.
Although the hotel has been open for 10 years, the maintenance of the guest rooms is still good. The overall style is still dark-toned and old-fashioned. The reception area is in the middle. The welcome gift includes a super large fruit plate, luggage tag, Qin terracotta warriors and other souvenirs, as well as a handwritten welcome card. In addition, there is a more detailed turndown service, and a shadow play ornament as a souvenir, which is better than the Hyatt next door.
.
The mini bar is relatively hidden. It is opened from the large cabinet in the living room. There is a capsule coffee machine with 6 capsules, tg tea bags, free water, which is rare in Kunlun Mountain, and a small refrigerator full of drinks and snacks, but they are charged. In terms of the configuration of the mini bar, it is also in line with the luxury brand standard, slightly better than Hyatt.
.
The bedroom and the living room are connected by sliding doors on both sides. The area is spacious. There is a bedside bench and a sofa by the window. There are green plants. The bedding is comfortable and tidy, which is in line with the luxury brand positioning. Going inside is a fully glass-clad, very transparent master bathroom. Opposite is a large independent cloakroom.
.
The shower room also puts a bathtub in it. Although I don‚Äôt like this design, fortunately the space is large enough. The bathtub is Villeroy & Boch, which is large and deep, and the body feels comfortable. The shower system is Hansgrohe, and the spare parts 50ml Yuebishi are very good.
.
The washbasin is not spacious, but the basin is interesting. The double faucet shares a large one-piece basin. The main bathroom uses the same Villeroy & Boch hanging toilet as the guest bathroom. There is no smart toilet cover installed, but considering that it is a 14-year-old hotel, it is understandable.
.
The room service is very good and the response is very fast. Almost as soon as I put down the phone, the things I needed were delivered. The service level of this hotel is first-class, whether it is the concierge, front desk, lounge or room service. I would like to specially praise the handsome brother STAYME7O in the lounge for providing proactive and elegant service.
.
In general, the space is very good, the area is large, the configuration is upscale, and the cost performance is very high. I am really satisfied to live in such a suite at the price of Hyatt's basic room.

name:w‚Äçi‚Äçn‚Äçn‚Äçe‚Äçy
info:Deluxe Twin
info:Stayed in July 2021
info:Family
info:2 Reviews
rating:2.5
posted:Posted July 29, 2021
msg:This is a very funny hotel. There is no concierge at the door, and no one takes luggage. We have three rooms. After check-in, we will have afternoon tea. Because we are with our children, we asked for an extra cup to share with the children. It was already taken to us. A waitress came to us and told us not to give us more cups and let us buy another afternoon tea. Can't we share 6 cups of tea in three rooms and one child to drink? In order not to affect our mood on the journey, we endured it. I received a call the next day asking if there were any shortcomings in the hotel. We responded one by one. The hotel manager wanted to give us breakfast the next day in order to thank us. The next day I checked out and I didn't see the fruit delivered... The sanitation of the hotel was not very good, and the room had an unpleasant smell when it entered. It was a world of difference from the first hotel we stayed in.
